Message: I'll analyze this Job Shop Scheduling Problem (JSSP) and create an initial schedule considering the precedence constraints within each job.

## Problem Analysis
- 20 jobs, each with 15 operations
- 15 machines (Machine0 through Machine14)
- Each job has strict precedence constraints (operations must be performed sequentially)
- Numbers in parentheses represent processing times

## Scheduling Strategy
I'll use a simple dispatching rule approach:
1. **Earliest Start Time (EST)** for each operation
2. **First Come First Serve (FCFS)** when multiple operations compete for the same machine
3. Respect precedence constraints within each job
